# <a name="azure-guest-os"></a><span data-ttu-id="ef89e-103">Azure 게스트 OS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ef89e-103">Azure Guest OS</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ef89e-104">다음 테이블에서 Azure 게스트 OS에 적용된 Microsoft 보안 대응 센터(MSRC) 업데이트를 보여줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ef89e-104">The following tables show the Microsoft Security Response Center (MSRC) updates applied to the Azure Guest OS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ef89e-105">사용 중인 게스트 OS에 특정 업데이트가 적용되는 경우 이 문서를 검색합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ef89e-105">Search this article to determine if a particular update applies to the Guest OS you are using.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ef89e-106">도입된 특정 [제품군][family-explain] 설명에 업데이트가 항상 수행됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ef89e-106">Updates always carry forward for the particular [family][family-explain] they were introduced in.</span></span>
